  33‚Üí## Architecture Overview\n    34‚Üí\n    35‚Üí### AI Workflow System\n    36‚ÜíThe core feature is a JSON-based workflow system where each workflow:\n    37‚Üí- Lives in `src/workflows/[workflow-name]/workflow.json`\n    38‚Üí- Contains multiple stages with prompts in `prompts/` subdirectory\n    39‚Üí- Each stage can specify its own AI model, temperature, and (`src/components/wizard/wizard-shell.tsx`): Main UI for workflow execution\n    44‚Üí- **AI Stage Execution** (`src/ai/flows/ai-stage-execution.ts`): Core AI processing logic using Genkit\n    45‚Üí- **Workflow Loader** (`src/lib/workflow-loader.ts`): Dynamic workflow loading system\n    46‚Üí\n    47‚Üí### Frontend Stack\n    48‚Üí- Next.js 15 with App Router\n    49‚Üí- TypeScript with path alias `@/*` for src imports\n    50‚Üí- Tailwind CSS with shadcn/ui components (Radix UI primitives)\n    51‚Üí- React Hook Form for form handling\n    52‚Üí- React Dropzone for file uploads\n    53‚Üí\n    54‚Üí### AI Integration\n    55‚Üí- **MIGRATION IN PROGRESS**: Moving from Google Genkit to native @google/genai SDK (branch: `backup/genkit-to-genai-attempt-1`)\n    56‚Üí- Primary model: 2.5)\n    61‚Üí  - Enhanced AI logging at `logs/ai.log`\n    62‚Üí- Supports multiple input types: textarea, form, context, none\n    63‚Üí- Output formats: text, json, markdown\n    64‚Üí\n we FAIL EARLY, we FAIL LOUD, we FAIL HARD!\n    72‚Üí- Never use mock data or fallback responses when AI fails\n    73‚Üí- NO FALLBACK LOGIC - if something fails, let it fail completely\n    74‚Üí- NO DEFENSIVE CODING - don't try to handle every edge case\n    75‚Üí- Always propagate errors to the user with clear error messages\n    76‚Üí- Log ALL errors with full stack traces\n    77‚Üí- This The form data must be saved to state before dependent stages can run.');\n    36‚Üí    }\n    37‚Üí  }\n    38‚Üí  \n    39‚Üí  // Deep clone the settings to avoid mutations\n    40‚Üí  const resolvedSettings = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(settings));\n    41‚Üí  \n    42‚Üí  // Helper function to resolve template variables\n    43‚Üí  const resolveTemplate = (template: string): string => {\n    44‚Üí    if (typeof template !== 'string') return template;\n    45‚Üí    \n    46‚Üí    const regex = /\\{\\{([\\w.-]+)\\}\\}/g;\n    47‚Üí    let result = template;\n    48‚Üí    let match;\n    49‚Üí    \n    50‚Üí    while ((match = regex.exec(template)) !== null) {\n    51‚Üí      const fullPath = match[1];\n    52‚Üí      const pathParts = fullPath.split('.');\n    53‚Üí      \n    54‚Üí      let value = contextVars;\n    55‚Üí      let found = true;\n    56‚Üí      for (const part of pathParts) {\n    57‚Üí        if (value && typeof value === 'object' && part in value) {\n    58‚Üí          value = value[part];\n    59‚Üí        } else {\n    60‚Üí          found = false;\n    61‚Üí          break;\n    62‚Üí        }\n    63‚Üí      }\n    64‚Üí      \n    65‚Üí      if (found) {\n    66‚Üí        const replacement = (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) ? JSON.stringify(value) : String(value);\n    67‚Üí        result = result.replace(match[0], replacement);\n    68‚Üí      } else {\n    69‚Üí        console.error(`Image generation template variable '{{${fullPath}}}' not found in context.`, {\n    70‚Üí          fullPath,\n    71‚Üí          contextVars,\n    72‚Üí          availableKeys: Object.keys(contextVars).map(k => `${k}: ${Object.keys(contextVars[k] || {}).join(', ')}`)\n    73‚Üí        });\n    74‚Üí        // Don't replace if not found, leave the template\n    75‚Üí      }\n    76‚Üí    }\n    77‚Üí    \n    78‚Üí    return result;\n    79‚Üí  };\n    80‚Üí  \n    81‚Üí  // Resolve aspectRatio and numberOfImages if they are template strings\n    82‚Üí  if (resolvedSettings.aspectRatio) {\n    83‚Üí    const resolved = resolveTemplate(resolvedSettings.aspectRatio);\n    84‚Üí    // FAIL HARD: If template variables aren't resolved, throw error\n    85‚Üí    if (resolved.includes('{{')) {\n    86‚Üí      throw new Error(`FATAL: Template variable '${resolvedSettings.aspectRatio}' could not be resolved. Required context data is missing.`);\n    87‚Üí    }\n    88‚Üí    // Validate that the aspect ratio is one of the supported values\n    89‚Üí    const validAspectRatios = ['1:1', '3:4', '4:3', '9:16', '16:9'];\n    90‚Üí    if (!validAspectRatios.includes(resolved)) {\n    91‚Üí      throw new Error(`FATAL: Invalid aspect ratio '${resolved}'. Must be one of: ${validAspectRatios.join(', ')}`);\n    92‚Üí    }\n    93‚Üí    resolvedSettings.aspectRatio = resolved;\n    94‚Üí  }\n    95‚Üí  \n    96‚Üí  if (resolvedSettings.numberOfImages) {\n    97‚Üí    const resolved = resolveTemplate(resolvedSettings.numberOfImages);\n    98‚Üí    // FAIL HARD: If template variables aren't resolved, throw error\n    99‚Üí    if (resolved.includes('{{')) {\n   100‚Üí      throw new Error(`FATAL: Template variable '${resolvedSettings.numberOfImages}' could not be resolved. Required context data is missing.`);\n   101‚Üí    }\n   102‚Üí    const numValue = parseInt(resolved, 10);\n   103‚Üí    if (isNaN(numValue) || numValue < 1 || numValue > 4) {\n   104‚Üí      throw new Error(`FATAL: Invalid numberOfImages '${resolved}'. Must be a number between 1 and 4.`);\n   105‚Üí    }\n   106‚Üí    resolvedSettings.numberOfImages = numValue;\n   107‚Üí  }\n   108‚Üí  \n   109‚Üí  // Resolve filenames from template context\n   110‚Üí  if (resolvedSettings.filenames) {\n   111‚Üí    const resolved = resolveTemplate(resolvedSettings.filenames);\n   112‚Üí    // FAIL HARD: If template variables aren't resolved, throw error\n   113‚Üí    if (resolved.includes('{{')) {\n   114‚Üí      throw new Error(`FATAL: Template variable '${resolvedSettings.filenames}' could not be resolved. AI-generated filenames not available.`);\n   115‚Üí    }\n   116‚Üí    \n   117‚Üí    try {\n   118‚Üí      // Parse the JSON array of filenames\n   119‚Üí      const parsedFilenames = JSON.parse(resolved);\n   120‚Üí      if (Array.isArray(parsedFilenames)) {\n   121‚Üí        resolvedSettings.filenames = parsedFilenames;\n   122‚Üí        console.log('[resolveImageGenerationSettings] Using AI-generated filenames:', parsedFilenames);\n   123‚Üí      } else {\n   124‚Üí        console.warn('[resolveImageGenerationSettings] Filenames is not an array, ignoring:', resolved);\n   125‚Üí        delete resolvedSettings.filenames;\n   126‚Üí      }\n   127‚Üí    } catch (parseError) {\n   128‚Üí      console.warn('[resolveImageGenerationSettings] Failed to parse filenames JSON, ignoring:', resolved);\n   129‚Üí      delete resolvedSettings.filenames;\n   130‚Üí    }\n   131‚Üí  }\n   132‚Üí  \n   133‚Üí  return resolvedSettings;\n   134‚Üí}\n   135‚Üí\n   136‚Üíinterface WizardShellProps {\n   137‚Üí  initialInstance: WizardInstance;\n   138‚Üí}\n   139‚Üí\n   140‚Üíexport function 146‚Üí  const [aiLoadError, setAiLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n   147‚Üí  const [aiLoadAttempts, setAiLoadAttempts] = useState(0);\n   148‚Üí  const [aiLoadStartTime, });\n   165‚Üí    \n   166‚Üí    try {\n   167‚Üí      const aiModule = await import('@/lib/ai-stage-runner');\n   168‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   169‚Üí      \n   170‚Üí    \n   187‚Üí      console.log('[WizardShell] ‚úÖ AI stage runner function validated successfully');\n   188‚Üí      \n   189‚Üí    } catch (error: any) {\n   190‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   191‚Üí      const errorDetails = {\n   192‚Üí        loadTimeMs: loadTime,\n   193‚Üí        attempt: retryAttempt + 1,\n   194‚Üí        errorMessage: error.message,\n   195‚Üí        errorStack: error.stack,\n   196‚Üí        errorName: error.name,\n   197‚Üí        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n   198‚Üí        userAgent: navigator.userAgent,\n   199‚Üí        url: \n   204‚Üí      console.error('[WizardShell] ‚ùå Failed to load AI stage runner:', errorDetails);\n   205‚Üí      \n   206‚Üí      setAiLoadAttempts(retryAttempt + 1);\n   207‚Üí      setAiLoadError(error.message);\n   208‚Üí      \n   209‚Üí      // Auto-retry up to 3 times with exponential backoff\n   210‚Üí      if (retryAttempt < 2) {\n   211‚Üí        const retryDelay = need to show toast for automatic retries\n   215‚Üí        \n   216‚Üí        setTimeout(() => {\n   217‚Üí          loadAiStageRunner(retryAttempt + 1);\n   218‚Üí        }, retryDelay);\n   219‚Üí      } else {\n   220‚Üí        // Final failure - show comprehensive error toast\n   221‚Üí        const comprehensiveError = `AI Module Load Failed After ${retryAttempt + 1} Attempts\n   222‚Üí\n   223‚Üíüîç Technical Details:\n   224‚Üí‚Ä¢ Error: ${error.message}\n   225‚Üí‚Ä¢ Load time: ${loadTime}ms\n   226‚Üí‚Ä¢ Network: ${navigator.onLine ? Refresh the page (Cmd/Ctrl + R)\n   237‚Üí2. Clear browser cache (Cmd/Ctrl + Shift + R)\n   238‚Üí3. Check browser console for more details\n   239‚Üí4. Try a different browser\n   240‚Üí5. Check network connection`;\n   241‚Üí\n   242‚Üí        toast({\n   243‚Üí          title: \"AI System Unavailable\",\n   244‚Üí          description: comprehensiveError,\n   245‚Üí          variant: \"destructive\",\n   246‚Üí          duration: 15000, // Show longer for complex error\n   247‚Üí          action: (\n   248‚Üí            <Button\n   249‚Üí              onClick={() => {\n   250‚Üí                setAiStageLoaded(false);\n   251‚Üí                setAiLoadError(null);\n   252‚Üí                setAiLoadAttempts(0);\n   253‚Üí                loadAiStageRunner();\n   254‚Üí              }}\n   255‚Üí              size=\"sm\"\n   256‚Üí            >\n   257‚Üí              Retry\n   258‚Üí            </Button>\n   259‚Üí          )\n   260‚Üí        });\n   261‚Üí      }\n   262‚Üí    }\n   263‚Üí  }, [toast, aiStageLoaded]);\n   264‚Üí\n   265‚Üí  // Load the AI stage runner dynamically with retries\n   266‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   267‚Üí    loadAiStageRunner();\n   268‚Üí  }, [loadAiStageRunner]);\n   269‚Üí\n   270‚Üí  // Auto-scroll utility\n   271‚Üí  const scrollToStageById = useCallback((stageId: string) => {\n   272‚Üí    const stageElement = document.getElementById(`stage-${stageId}`);\n   273‚Üí    if (stageElement) {\n   274‚Üí      const elementTop = stageElement.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset;\n   275‚Üí      const headerOffset = 120; // Account for sticky header height + some padding\n   276‚Üí      window.scrollTo({\n   277‚Üí        top: elementTop - headerOffset,\n   278‚Üí        behavior: 'smooth'\n   279‚Üí      });\n   280‚Üí    }\n   281‚Üí  }, []);\n   282‚Üí\n   283‚Üí  // Callback to sync instance changes from persistence layer\n   284‚Üí  const updateInstanceForPersistence = useCallback((updates: Partial<WizardInstance>) => {\n   285‚Üí    setInstance(prev => ({ ...prev, ...updates }));\n   286‚Üí  }, []);\n   287‚Üí\n   288‚Üí  // Document persistence\n   289‚Üí  const { \n   290‚Üí    isSaving, \n   291‚Üí    lastSaved, \n   292‚Üí    saveError, \n   293‚Üí    documentId,\n   294‚Üí    saveDocument \n   295‚Üí  } = useDocumentPersistence({\n   296‚Üí    instance,\n   297‚Üí    updateInstance: updateInstanceForPersistence,\n   298‚Üí  });\n   299‚Üí\n   300‚Üí  const updateStageState = useCallback((stageId: string, updates: Partial<StageState>) => {\n   301‚Üí    let needsImmediateSave = false;\n   302‚Üí    const resultState = setInstance(prevInstance => {\n   303‚Üí      const newStageStates = {\n   304‚Üí        ...prevInstance.stageStates,\n   305‚Üí 321‚Üí\n   322‚Üí    if (needsImmediateSave) {\n   323‚Üí      // Next tick save so React state has committed\n   324‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {\n   325‚Üí        saveDocument();\n   326‚Üí      }, 0);\n   327‚Üí    }\n   328‚Üí  }, [saveDocument]);\n   329‚Üí\n   330‚Üí  // Enhanced dependency evaluation logic with support for autoRunConditions\n   331‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   332‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   333‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   334‚Üí\n   335‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   336‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   337‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   338‚Üí\n   339‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   340‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   341‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   342‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   343‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   344‚Üí        );\n   345‚Üí      }\n   346‚Üí\n   347‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   348‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   349‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   350‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   351‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   352‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   353‚Üí          );\n   354‚Üí        }\n   355‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   356‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   357‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   358‚Üí          );\n   359‚Üí        }\n   360‚Üí      }\n   361‚Üí      \n   362‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   363‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   364‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   365‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   366‚Üí        \n   367‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   368‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   369‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   370‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   371‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   372‚Üí          });\n   373‚Üí        }\n   374‚Üí        \n   375‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   376‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   377‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   378‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   379‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   380‚Üí          });\n   381‚Üí        }\n   382‚Üí        \n   383‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   384‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   385‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   386‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   387‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   388‚Üí          });\n   389‚Üí        }\n   390‚Üí      }\n   391‚Üí\n   392‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   393‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   394‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   395‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   396‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   397‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   398‚Üí        );\n   399‚Üí      } else {\n   400‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   401‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   402‚Üí      }\n   403‚Üí\n   404‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   405‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   406‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   407‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   408‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   409‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   410‚Üí        } else {\n   411‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   412‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   413‚Üí        }\n   414‚Üí      }\n   415‚Üí\n   416‚Üí      if (\n   417‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   418‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   419‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   420‚Üí      ) {\n   421‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   422‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   423‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   424‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   425‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   426‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   427‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   428‚Üí        };\n   429‚Üí        changed = true;\n   430‚Üí      }\n   431‚Üí    });\n   432‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   433‚Üí  };\n   434‚Üí  \n   435‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   436‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   437‚Üí    setInstance(prevInstance => ({\n   438‚Üí      ...prevInstance,\n   439‚Üí      stageStates: evaluateDependenciesLogic(prevInstance.stageStates, prevInstance.workflow.stages)\n   440‚Üí    }));\n   441‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   442‚Üí\n   443‚Üí\n   444‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   445‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   446‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   447‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   448‚Üí      if (stageState && stageState.shouldAutoRun && stageState.status === 'idle' && stageState.depsAreMet && !stageState.isEditingOutput) {\n   449‚Üí        console.log(`[Autorun] Triggering autorun for stage ${stage.id}`);\n   450‚Üí        handleRunStage(stage.id, stageState.userInput);\n   451‚Üí      }\n   452‚Üí    });\n   453‚Üí    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n   454‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   455‚Üí\n   456‚Üí\n   457‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   458‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   459‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   460‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   461‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n   462‚Üí        let newTitle = \"\";\n   463‚Üí        if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') {\n   464‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   465‚Üí        } \n   466‚Üí  } else {\n        console.warn('[resolveImageGenerationSettings] Filenames is not an array, ignoring:', resolved);\n        delete resolvedSettings.filenames;\n      }\n    } catch (parseError) {\n
